Here are some symptoms:\n   528→      #   * Calling nvidia-smi timeouts after 60 second\n   529→      #   * Fail to run nvidia-smi with an unable to determine the device handle for GPU\n   530→      #     unknown error\n   531→      #   * Test fails with a missing CUDA GPU error when initializing CUDA in PyTorch\n   532→      #   * Run docker --gpus all fails with error response from daemon\n   533→      #\n   534→      # As both the root cause and recovery path are unclear, let's take the runner out of\n   535→      # service so that it doesn't get any more jobs\n   536→      - name: Check NVIDIA driver installation step\n   537→        if: failure() && steps.install-nvidia-driver.outputs.has-nvidia == 'true' && !contains(matrix.runner, 'b200')\n   538→        shell: bash\n   539→        run: |\n   540→          set +e\n   541→          set -x\n   542→\n   543→          nvidia-smi\n   544→          # NB: Surprisingly, nvidia-smi command returns successfully with return code 0 even in\n   545→          # the case where the driver has already crashed as it still can get the driver version\n   546→          # and some basic information like the bus ID.  However, the rest of the information\n   547→          # would be missing (ERR!), for example:\n   548→          #\n   549→          # +-----------------------------------------------------------------------------+\n   550→          # | NVIDIA-SMI 525.89.02    Driver Version: 525.89.02    CUDA Version: 12.0     |\n   551→          # |-------------------------------+----------------------+----------------------+\n   552→          # | GPU  Name        Persistence-M| Bus-Id        Disp.A | Volatile Uncorr.
